          <h3 class="c-heading-5 ow-pb-05 ow-no-padding-top x-weight-semibold ow-slide-in ow-slide-in-2 ow-headinghelper-2">Call from Teams, Outlook, or a mobile device</h3>

       <div class="ow-standalone-sku-right"> 
        <div class="ow-standalone-flex-container"> 
         <h3 class="c-paragraph-3 x-weight-semibold ow-tal ow-headinghelper-2" dir="ltr">Microsoft 365 Business Voice includes:</h3> 
         <div class="ow-authoring-container"> 
          <ul class="c-list"> 
           <li>Cloud-based phone system with advanced features including call transfer, multilevel auto attendants, and call queues.</li> 
           <li>A domestic calling plan with 3,000 minutes<sup><a aria-label="Footnote 2" class="c-hyperlink" href="#office-CustomSpacingTemplate-ky9uhze">2</a></sup> per user, per month within the US and Canada.</li> 
           <li>Dial-in audio conferencing for up to 250 people per meeting.</li> 
           <li>Call from anywhere, on any device through the Microsoft Teams app on desktop, mobile, web, and desk phones.</li> 
           <li>Around-the-clock customer support seven days a week, backed by Microsoft.</li> 
          </ul> 
          <p>&nbsp;</p> 
          <p>Business Voice requires a Microsoft 365 subscription that includes Microsoft Teams.<sup><a aria-label="Footnote 4" class="c-hyperlink" href="#office-CustomSpacingTemplate-ky9uhze">3</a></sup>&nbsp;Its an add-on subscription for up to 300 users and cant be used on its own. Business Voice add-on and trial are only available for users with qualifying plans.</p> 
          <p>&nbsp;</p> 
          <p>Discounted pricing valid up to 12 months or up to the renewal date of the base M365 subscription. Price available now through June 30, 2021.<a class="c-hyperlink" href="#office-CustomSpacingTemplate-ky9uhze"><sup>6</sup></a></p> 
          <p>&nbsp;</p> 
          <p>Price includes required communication taxes and fees.<sup><a aria-label="Footnote 1" class="c-hyperlink" href="#office-CustomSpacingTemplate-ky9uhze">1</a></sup></p>

    <div id="office-CustomSpacingTemplate-v5dq4rp" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;addResourcesspacer 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_office-CustomSpacingTemplate&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m1r13a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r13a2&quot;}" data-module-id="Office.ScenarioTemplate|additionalresourcesregion|coreui-region|office-CustomSpacingTemplate-v5dq4rp|office-CustomSpacingTemplate">

   <div id="additionalResourcesFaqsRegion" data-grid="container" data-region-key="additionalresourcesfaqsregion" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;additionalResourcesFaqsRegion 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Region_coreui-region&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;r14a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:14,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;a2&quot;}"> 
    <div id="coreui-heading-p4wboop" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;arfaqsHeading 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-heading&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m1r14a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r14a2&quot;}" data-module-id="Office.ScenarioTemplate|additionalResourcesFaqsRegion|coreui-region|coreui-heading-p4wboop|coreui-heading"> 
     <header role="presentation" class="m-heading-2"> 
      <h2 class="c-heading-3">Frequently asked questions</h2> 
     </header> 
    </div> 
    <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;arFaqs 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-collapsibledrawer&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m2r14a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:2,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r14a2&quot;}" data-module-id="Office.ScenarioTemplate|additionalResourcesFaqsRegion|coreui-region|coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb|coreui-collapsibledrawer"> 
     <section class="cui-drawer"> 
      <div class="cui-header f-divider"> 
       <div class="cui-drawer-toggle"> <button data-m="{&quot;pid&quot;:&quot;Expand all&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn1m2r14a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r14a2&quot;}" class="f-expand c-action-toggle" name="Expand all" data-toggled-label="Expand all" aria-label="Expand all">Expand all</button> <span>|</span> <button data-m="{&quot;pid&quot;:&quot;Collapse all&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn2m2r14a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:2,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r14a2&quot;}" class="f-collapse c-action-toggle" name="Collapse all" data-toggled-label="Collapse all" aria-label="Collapse all" disabled>Collapse all</button> 
       </div> 
       <div style="clear: both;"></div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn3m2r14a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:3,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r14a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer0">What is Microsoft Teams Calling?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer0" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Microsoft Teams Calling refers to the capability of people to make and receive calls in Microsoft Teams. Microsoft 365 subscriptions including Teams Calling from one Teams app to another Teams app. Making and receiving calls to and from landlines and mobile phones on the public switch telephone network (PSTN) in Teams is available with an add-on like Microsoft 365 Business Voice or is included in Microsoft 365 E5. These options provide a cloud-based phone system in Teams with features such as hold, blind and safe transfers, and reporting features for professionals who manage calling solutions.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn4m2r14a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:4,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r14a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer1">What is a Microsoft Teams Calling Plan?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer1" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>A calling plan provides users with a primary phone number and calling minutes to make and receive phone calls. A domestic calling plan is included in Business Voice or can be added onto Microsoft 365 E5.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn5m2r14a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:5,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r14a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer2">What is Direct Routing?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer2" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Direct Routing allows customers to connect their telecom voice trunks directly to Microsoft 365 so people can make and receive calls. Customers can work with their local telecommunications provider to connect their voice trunks through a certified session border controller (SBC) to Microsoft 365 and Microsoft Teams Calling. This will be available in any country where Microsoft Teams and the phone system are licensed. Direct Routing is part of the Teams-compatible phone system.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn6m2r14a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:6,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r14a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer3">What is the difference between the offers for small and medium-sized businesses and enterprises?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer3" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>There are two offers for small and medium-sized businesses. Microsoft 365 Business Voice with a calling plan combines a phone system, audio conferencing, and a domestic calling plan. Microsoft 365 Business Voice without a calling plan combines a phone system and audio conferencing, which requires a calling plan from a service provider.</p> 
        <p>&nbsp;</p> 
        <p>For enterprises: A phone system and audio conferencing are included in Office 365 E5 and Microsoft 365 E5. Microsoft Teams Calling Plans can be added on, or they can all be purchased separately.</p> 
        <p>&nbsp;</p> 
        <p>Business Voice with a calling plan is currently available in the US, UK, and Canada. Calling plans are available for enterprises in the US, UK, and Canada as well as Belgium, France, Germany, Ireland, Netherlands, Puerto Rico, and Spain. Business Voice without a calling plan is available in over 70 countries, everywhere audio conferencing is available. A phone system for enterprises is available in over 120 countries, everywhere Microsoft 365 is available.</p> 
        <p>&nbsp;</p> 
        <p>The product features and experience are the same across the offers for small and medium-sized businesses and enterprises. Pricing and availability differ.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn7m2r14a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:7,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r14a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer4">What is Microsoft 365 Business Voice?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer4" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Microsoft 365 Business Voice is a cloud-based phone system built for small and medium-sized businesses. It enables users to make, receive, and transfer calls to and from landlines and mobile phones on the public switched telephone network (PSTN) in Microsoft Teams.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn8m2r14a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:8,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r14a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer5">Who is Microsoft 365 Business Voice intended for?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer5" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Its designed for small and medium-sized businesses using Microsoft 365 that are seeking a modern phone system. Business Voice can be added onto Microsoft 365 subscriptions that include Microsoft Teams; qualifying plans include Microsoft 365 Business Basic, Business Standard, Business Premium, E3, or A3; Office 365 F3, E1, E3, A1, or A3. You can purchase up to 300 seats of Business Voice. If your company has more than 300 users,&nbsp;<a aria-label="Learn more about voice calling solutions on the Microsoft Teams page." class="c-hyperlink" href="https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/microsoft-teams/voice-calling">learn more about our Enterprise Voice solution</a>.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn9m2r14a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:9,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r14a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer6">Whats included in Microsoft 365 Business Voice?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer6" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Business Voice includes a phone system, a domestic calling plan, and audio conferencing. <a aria-label="Learn more about Business Voice" class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=2141577">Learn more</a>.</p> 
        <p>&nbsp;</p> 
        <p>A prepaid wallet (known as <a aria-label="Learn more about communications credits in Microsoft Teams" class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=2141636">Communications Credits</a>) is available for adding toll-free, additional minutes, and other pay-per-minute charges.</p> 
        <p>An optional international calling plan that includes 600 minutes per user per month can be purchased as an add-on to Business Voice.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn10m2r14a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:10,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r14a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer7">Where is Microsoft 365 Business Voice available?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer7" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Businesses operating in the US, UK, and Canada can purchase Business Voice. In other countries, Business Voice may be available through Microsoft partners who provide dial tone services.&nbsp;<a aria-label="Find a Microsoft partner in your area on the solutions provider search page on the Microsoft website" class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=2141975">Find a Microsoft partner in your area</a>.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn11m2r14a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:11,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r14a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer8">Where can I learn more about Microsoft 365 Business Voice?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer8" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>You can learn how to plan, set up, and use Business Voice <a aria-label="Learn more about Microsoft 365 Business voice on the Microsoft 365 Business Voice documentation page" class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=2141775">on the Microsoft 365 Business Voice documentation page</a>.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn12m2r14a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:12,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r14a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer9">Can I use my existing phone numbers?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer9" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Yes, you can <a aria-label="Learn how to transfer your phone numbers to Microsoft Teams Calling Plans." class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=2141833">transfer your phone numbers</a> from your current service provider. After you port your phone numbers over, Microsoft will become your service provider.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn13m2r14a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:13,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r14a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer10">Can I bring my own calling plan?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer10" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Yes, customers can work with their Microsoft partner to bring their own calling plan. A configuration called <a aria-label="Read more about direct routing" class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=2141637">Direct Routing</a> allows customers to connect voice trunks directly from their network to Microsoft Teams or interconnect other telephony entities such as call centers or analog devices.</p> 
        <p>&nbsp;</p> 
        <p>The Microsoft 365 Business Voice subscription (without a calling plan) is specifically designed for this situation and is <a aria-label="See country and region availability for audio conferencing and calling plans" class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=2141834">available</a> in over 70 countries, except Australia. Contact your partner and ask them if they're&nbsp;offering it. If you don't have a Microsoft partner, you can&nbsp;<a aria-label="Find a partner on the Microsoft website" class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=2090502">find a partner on the Microsoft website</a>.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn14m2r14a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:14,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r14a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer11">What phones are supported?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer11" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Microsoft 365 Business Voice is experienced through the Microsoft Teams apps. Devices certified for Teams provide&nbsp;a seamless Teams experience on desk phones, conference phones, and meeting room systems.&nbsp;<a aria-label="Learn more about Microsoft Teams certified devices." class="c-hyperlink" href="https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/microsoft-teams/across-devices">Learn more about Microsoft Teams certified devices</a>. For available devices check out the <a aria-label="See available devices in the Microsoft Teams Devices Marketplace." class="c-hyperlink" href="https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/microsoft-teams/across-devices/devices">Microsoft Teams Devices Marketplace</a>.</p> 
        <p>&nbsp;</p> 
        <p>Business Voice works with devices certified for Skype for Business with features in <a aria-label="Learn more in this list about Skype for Business certified devices compatible with Business Voice" class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=2141836">this list</a>. In 2023, these devices will no longer work with Business Voice.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn15m2r14a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:15,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r14a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer12">Where can I share thoughts and ideas?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-xyh6yvb-collapsible-drawer12" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Got a suggestion? Wed love to hear from you. Here are three ways to share feedback:</p> 
        <ul class="c-list"> 
         <li>Microsoft Teams desktop app. Click Help on the bottom left. Then click Report a problem or Suggest a feature.</li> 
         <li><a aria-label="Submit ideas and vote on others ideas on the Microsoft UserVoice site." class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=2141837">UserVoice</a>  Submit and vote on others ideas.</li> 
         <li><a aria-label="Ask questions and join discussions in the Microsoft Tech Community." class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=2141638">Microsoft Tech Community</a>  Ask questions and join discussions.</li> 
        </ul> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </section> 
    </div>
